MOD_NAME=Enhanced Tactical Info
AUTHOR=eclipse666
DESCRIPTION=Displays soldier XP/PsiXP, mobility, damage reduction and active/killed alien counts on the soldier info screen during battle (F1). XP values take mission completion bonuses into account. 
XP earned for each kill will now briefly appear above the killed alien (e.g. "+22XP")

/*
VERSIONS
1.0a - Initial release
1.0b - Updated to take dynamic war settings into account (mission bonus xp is nor correctly scaled according to dynamic war setting)
1.0c - Updated so that the "Trooper X has earned a promotion" message now also takes mission bonus xp into account.
1.0d - Active alien counts are now displayed under the soldier's name. Added current damage reduction value to soldier stats.
1.0e - Active alien counts should now also display when a SHIV is selected. 
       Tweaked DR calculation to remove randomness when used with this mod (does not affect the rest of the game). DR value displayed will now be the minimum.
1.0f - Version that treated critical wounds as dead soldiers - was removed
1.0g - XP for covert operative now also taken into account.
       DR value calculation updated. It would display very large values when percentage based DR was in use (e.g. by MECs). If % based DR in in use then it
       will now display the amount of damage that will be absorbed for an incoming damage value of 12.
1.0h - Aliens killed count now appears next to active alien counts. 
       XP earned from each kill will now appear on screen over the dead alien (e.g. +22XP)

This mod displays a soldier's XP, Psi XP, mobility, damage reduction and active alien counts on the soldier information screen during battle (F1). Psi XP is only displayed for
soldiers with Psi Rank > 0. The text labels (Health, Will, etc) have been replaced with icons so the screen looks nicer too.

Unlike other similar mods that display soldier XP, this version takes into account any bonus XP that the soldier will qualify for when the mission completes
so the "level up" indicator (the plus "+" sign to the left of the soldier's name) on the main battlefield HUD will light up correctly if the soldier will 
be promoted at the end of the mission. You no longer have to guess if a rookie will get promoted or not. Any PsiXP mission completion bonuses are included as well.

A count of active aliens for each alien type is displayed under the soldier's name. An alien becomes active once it makes contact with the squad. Now you can be
sure that you've completely cleared out a pod of aliens.

The bonus XP calculation uses the same internal functions used by the game so it is very accurate. 
The damage reduction value displayed is calculated by calling the game's internal AbsorbDamage function.

Bonus XP (awarded at the end of the mission) is calculated as follows:

STANDARD MISSIONS
 - Mission Complete: +80 xp
 - Soldier saw a "special" alien (e.g. Outsider): +30xp

 - SPECIAL MISSIONS (e.g. Council missions, etc).
 - Mission Complete: +120 xp
 - Soldier saw a "high level" alien (e.g. Outsider): +60xp

 - No soldiers died on the mission: +20xp
   (note that if a soldier dies on the mission then the bonus will automatically subtract this 20xp on the display)
   
COVERT EXTRACTIONS
 - Covert operative gets an additional +120xp

Any special items or effects are also taken into account (e.g. extra XP for officers with medals that add bonus XP, etc.)

*/

//This script was generated by HexToPseudoCode decompiler for use with PatchUPK/PatcherGUI tool
